730<script>

731 // Get the modal

732 $(document).ready(function(){

733 var params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);

734 var startDate = new Date("2021-10-25T00:05:00.000-08:00");

735 var endDate = new Date('2021-10-31T23:30:00.000-08:00');

736 var td = new Date();

737 var acode = 'halloween21';

738 if(params.get('preview') == acode || (td > startDate && td < endDate)) {

739 $('.topbar-announcement').addClass('is-open');

740 $('.site-header.is-standard').css('top', 90);

741 $('.site-header.is-hamburger').css('top', 110);

742 $('.acode').html(acode.toUpperCase());

743 }

744

745 $('.btn-close-panel').on('click', function(e){

746 e.preventDefault();

747 $('.topbar-announcement').removeClass('is-open');

748 $('.site-header.is-hamburger').css('top', '');

749 $('.site-header.is-standard').css('top', '');

750 });

753 e.preventDefault();

754 $('#announcement-modal').addClass('is-open');

755 });

756

757 $('#announcement-modal [data-dismiss="modal"]').on('click', function(e){

758 e.preventDefault();

759 $('#announcement-modal').removeClass('is-open');

760 });

761 })
